      function getStubClassName(targetClassName)
      {
        var stubs = {};
        stubs['xdo.app.System'] = "xdo.stub.bip.SystemIO";
        stubs['xdo.io.Catalog'] = "xdo.stub.bip.CatalogIO";
        stubs['xdo.io.Zip'] = "xdo.stub.bip.ZipIO";
        return stubs[targetClassName];
      }
